\arxivwithtarget{2603.16356}{Toward Experimentation-as-a-Service in 5G/6G: The Plaza6G Prototype for AI-Assisted Trials}{Sergio Barrachina-Muñoz, Marc Carrascosa-Zamacois, Horacio Bleda, Umair Riaz, Yasir Maqsood, Xavier Calle, Selva Vía, Miquel Payaró, Josep Mangues-Bafalluy}\textbf{cs.NI}, cs.AI.

本文介绍了首个可操作的Experiment-as-a-Service (ExaS)平台Plaza6G, 它将云资源与下一代无线基础设施统一起来. 该平台通过web门户或REST API支持自然语言实验设计, 并集成了基于LLM的助手, 采用retrieval-augmented generation (RAG)和Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA)技术进行知识增强与持续微调. 平台利用OTA测试设施和双站点室外5G网络进行演示, 实现了自动化CI/CD集成和可编程传播条件下的交互测试, 其机器可读的实验描述符确保了可重复性.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16357}{Beyond Grading Accuracy: Exploring Alignment of TAs and LLMs}{Matthijs Jansen op de Haar, Nacir Bouali, Faizan Ahmed}\textbf{cs.CY}, cs.SE.

本研究探讨了开源 Large Language Models (LLMs) 在评估 Unified Modeling Language (UML) 类图方面的潜力, 重点关注其与助教(TA)评分的对齐程度. 通过一个针对 92 个学生图表的定量研究, 作者在单个评分标准层面比较了六种开源 LLMs 与 TA 的评估结果, 发现最佳模型的 per-criterion accuracy 可达 88.56%, Pearson correlation coefficient 高达 0.78. 研究还提出了一个按标准组合最优 LLM 的“最优模型”, 其表现接近 TA 水平, 为构建混合主动评分系统提供了可能路径. 这些发现表明, 开源 LLMs 能有效支持 UML 图表评分, 并通过明确识别评分对齐来帮助管理日益增长的评估工作量.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16362}{$D^3$-RSMDE: 40$\times$ Faster and High-Fidelity Remote Sensing Monocular Depth Estimation}{Ruizhi Wang, Weihan Li, Zunlei Feng, Haofei Zhang, Mingli Song, Jiayu Wang, Jie Song, Li Sun}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16368}{Encoding Predictability and Legibility for Style-Conditioned Diffusion Policy}{Adrien Jacquet Crétides, Mouad Abrini, Hamed Rahimi, Mohamed Chetouani}\textbf{cs.RO}, cs.LG.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16384}{Controlling Fish Schools via Reinforcement Learning of Virtual Fish Movement}{Yusuke Nishii, Hiroaki Kawashima}\textbf{cs.RO}, cs.LG, q-bio.PE.

该研究提出了一种基于 reinforcement learning 的虚拟鱼控制方法, 用于引导真实鱼群运动. 通过 model-free 的 reinforcement learning 策略, 虚拟鱼能在模拟环境中学习有效的引导策略, 即使真实鱼对刺激响应不频繁. 实验验证了该策略在真实鱼群引导任务中的有效性, 其性能显著优于无刺激基准和启发式策略. 这项工作展示了 reinforcement learning 在通过人工智能体影响动物群体行为方面的潜力.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16393}{Robust Physics-Guided Diffusion for Full-Waveform Inversion}{Jishen Peng, Enze Jiang, Zheng Ma, Xiongbin Yan}\textbf{math.NA}, cs.AI.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16423}{SF-Mamba: Rethinking State Space Model for Vision}{Masakazu Yoshimura, Teruaki Hayashi, Yuki Hoshino, Wei-Yao Wang, Takeshi Ohashi}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16428}{An Efficient Heterogeneous Co-Design for Fine-Tuning on a Single GPU}{Ruijia Yang, Zeyi Wen}\textbf{cs.DC}, cs.AI.

SlideFormer 是一种针对单 GPU 环境的系统, 旨在解决 LLM 微调中的内存瓶颈问题. 其核心设计包括一个轻量级异步引擎, 将 GPU 视为滑动窗口, 并重叠 GPU 计算与 CPU 更新及多级 I/O. 该系统通过高效异构内存管理方案显著降低峰值内存使用, 并集成优化的 Triton kernels 以解决关键性能瓶颈. 这使得在单张 RTX 4090 GPU 上微调 123B+ 参数模型成为可能, 相比基线方法, 在吞吐量上实现了 1.40x 至 6.27x 的提升, 同时将 CPU/GPU 内存使用量减半.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16429}{LenghuSky-8: An 8-Year All-Sky Cloud Dataset with Star-Aware Masks and Alt-Az Calibration for Segmentation and Nowcasting}{Yicheng Rui, Xiao-Wei Duan, Licai Deng, Fan Yang, Zhengming Dang, Zhengjun Du, Junhao Peng, Wenhao Chu, Umut Mahmut, Kexin Li, Yiyun Wu, Fabo Feng}\textbf{astro-ph.IM}, cs.AI, cs.CV.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16432}{IRIS: A Real-World Benchmark for Inverse Recovery and Identification of Physical Dynamic Systems from Monocular Video}{Rasul Khanbayov, Mohamed Rayan Barhdadi, Erchin Serpedin, Hasan Kurban}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.LG.

该研究提出了首个用于从单目视频中无监督恢复和识别物理动态系统的真实世界基准IRIS. 该基准包含220个高保真视频, 涵盖单体和多体系统, 并提供了独立测量的ground-truth参数及其不确定性估计, 以及对应的governing equations. 研究定义了一个标准化的评估协议, 涵盖参数准确性, 可识别性, 外推性, 鲁棒性和控制方程选择等多个维度. 通过评估多种基线方法, 包括多步physics loss formulation和四种互补的equation-identification策略, 为未来研究建立了性能参考并揭示了系统性的失败模式.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16439}{CD-FKD: Cross-Domain Feature Knowledge Distillation for Robust Single-Domain Generalization in Object Detection}{Junseok Lee, Sungho Shin, Seongju Lee, Kyoobin Lee}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16470}{Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning Counteracts Delayed CSI in Multi-Satellite Systems}{Marios Aristodemou, Yasaman Omid, Sangarapillai Lambotharan, Mahsa Derakhshan, Lajos Hanzo}\textbf{cs.IT}, cs.AI, eess.SP.

该研究针对多卫星系统中因传播延迟导致的outdated CSI问题, 提出了一种名为dual stage proximal policy optimisation (DS-PPO)的MARL算法. 该方法通过双层优化结构处理连续动作空间与非独立同分布环境, 第一层优化单个卫星的sum-rate, 第二层协调所有卫星以最大化整体sum-rate. 数值结果表明, DS-PPO能有效对抗CSI不完美性并提升系统性能, 同时论文提供了算法的收敛性与复杂度分析.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16482}{DST-Net: A Dual-Stream Transformer with Illumination-Independent Feature Guidance and Multi-Scale Spatial Convolution for Low-Light Image Enhancement}{Yicui Shi, Yuhan Chen, Xiangfei Huang, Zhenguo Wang, Wenxuan Yu, Ying Fang}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16489}{Unlearning for One-Step Generative Models via Unbalanced Optimal Transport}{Hyundo Choi, Junhyeong An, Jinseong Park, Jaewoong Choi}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16524}{An approximate graph elicits detonation lattice}{Vansh Sharma, Venkat Raman}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.LG, physics.comp-ph, physics.data-an.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16549}{Bridging the Simulation-to-Reality Gap in Electron Microscope Calibration via VAE-EM Estimation}{Jilles S. van Hulst, W.P.M.H., Heemels, Duarte J. Antunes}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.LG.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16551}{CompDiff: Hierarchical Compositional Diffusion for Fair and Zero-Shot Intersectional Medical Image Generation}{Mahmoud Ibrahim, Bart Elen, Chang Sun, Gokhan Ertaylan, Michel Dumontier}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16565}{Deep Learning-Driven Black-Box Doherty Power Amplifier with Pixelated Output Combiner and Extended Efficiency Range}{Han Zhou, Haojie Chang, David Widen}\textbf{eess.SP}, cs.AI, cs.AR, eess.SY.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16576}{REFORGE: Multi-modal Attacks Reveal Vulnerable Concept Unlearning in Image Generation Models}{Yong Zou, Haoran Li, Fanxiao Li, Shenyang Wei, Yunyun Dong, Li Tang, Wei Zhou, Renyang Liu}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI, cs.CR, cs.LG.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16596}{FSMC-Pose: Frequency and Spatial Fusion with Multiscale Self-calibration for Cattle Mounting Pose Estimation}{Fangjing Li, Zhihai Wang, Xinxin Ding, Haiyang Liu, Ronghua Gao, Rong Wang, Yao Zhu, Ming Jin}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.

FSMC-Pose 提出了一种用于奶牛发情期姿态估计的 top-down 框架, 通过轻量级的频率-空间融合骨干网络 CattleMountNet 和多尺度自校准头 SC2Head 来处理复杂背景和动物间遮挡. 该方法设计了 SFEBlock 和 RABlock 来分离前景并捕获多尺度上下文信息, 同时引入自校准分支以缓解结构错位. 在结合 MOUNT-Cattle 和 NWAFU-Cattle 的数据集上, 该模型在保持实时推理的同时, 以更低的计算和参数成本实现了更高的准确率.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16599}{Data-driven generalized perimeter control: Zürich case study}{Alessio Rimoldi, Carlo Cenedese, Alberto Padoan, Florian Dörfler, John Lygeros}\textbf{eess.SY}, cs.AI, cs.CE, cs.ET.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16629}{MLLM-based Textual Explanations for Face Comparison}{Redwan Sony, Anil K Jain, Ross Arun}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.

本文系统评估了 MLLM 在无约束人脸验证任务中生成文本解释的可靠性, 重点关注极端姿态和监控图像. 研究发现, 即使 MLLM 做出正确验证决策, 其解释也常依赖无法验证或虚构的面部属性, 缺乏视觉证据支持. 引入传统 face recognition 系统的分数和决策信息虽能提升分类性能, 但并未持续改善解释的忠实性. 为此, 作者提出了一个基于 likelihood ratio 的评估框架 $L(x) = \frac{P(E|H_1)}{P(E|H_0)}$ 来衡量文本解释的证据强度, 揭示了当前 MLLM 在可解释人脸识别中的根本局限.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16663}{When Openclaw Agents Learn from Each Other: Insights from Emergent AI Agent Communities for Human-AI Partnership in Education}{Eason Chen, Ce Guan, Ahmed Elshafiey, Zhonghao Zhao, Joshua Zekeri, Afeez Edeifo Shaibu, Emmanuel Osadebe Prince, Cyuan-Jhen Wu}\textbf{cs.CY}, cs.AI, cs.HC, cs.MA.

该研究通过观察Moltbook等平台中大量AI agent的自主交互, 揭示了多agent系统在无预设课程下涌现的peer learning现象, 包括idea cascades和quality hierarchies. 研究发现人类在配置agent时经历"bidirectional scaffolding"过程, 而agent会自发形成类似open learner model的shared memory architectures. 这些自然现象为设计多agent教育系统提供了新视角, 例如"Learn by Teaching Your AI Agent Teammate"课程设计, 并指出了trust dynamics和platform mortality等设计约束.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16664}{Kestrel: Grounding Self-Refinement for LVLM Hallucination Mitigation}{Jiawei Mao, Hardy Chen, Haoqin Tu, Yuhan Wang, Letian Zhang, Zeyu Zheng, Huaxiu Yao, Zirui Wang, Cihang Xie, Yuyin Zhou}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.

Kestrel 提出了一种无需训练的框架, 用于缓解 LVLM 的幻觉问题. 该方法通过显式的视觉 grounding agent 收集结构化文本证据, 并利用 LVLM judge 进行验证. 基于验证后的证据, 模型通过迭代的 self-refinement 机制修正答案, 降低过校正风险. 实验表明, Kestrel 在多个幻觉基准上显著提升性能, 例如在 POPE 上平均提升 +3.31%, 同时提供可解释的验证轨迹.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16666}{Fast-WAM: Do World Action Models Need Test-time Future Imagination?}{Tianyuan Yuan, Zibin Dong, Yicheng Liu, Hang Zhao}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16673}{When Should a Robot Think? Resource-Aware Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning for Embodied Robotic Decision-Making}{Jun Liu, Pu Zhao, Zhenglun Kong, Xuan Shen, Peiyan Dong, Fan Yang, Lin Cui, Hao Tang, Geng Yuan, Wei Niu, Wenbin Zhang, Xue Lin, Gaowen Liu, Yanzhi Wang, Dong Huang}\textbf{cs.RO}, cs.AI, cs.LG.

本文提出了一种名为RARRL的分层框架, 旨在解决具身机器人系统中基于LLM的智能体在推理与执行之间的资源分配问题. 该框架通过强化学习训练一个高层编排策略, 使智能体能够根据当前观测、历史执行状态和剩余资源, 自适应地决定是否调用推理、选择何种推理角色以及分配多少计算预算. 实验表明, RARRL在ALFRED基准测试中显著提高了任务成功率, 同时降低了执行延迟并增强了系统鲁棒性. 这证明了自适应推理控制对于构建高效可靠的具身机器人智能体至关重要.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16712}{High-dimensional estimation with missing data: Statistical and computational limits}{Kabir Aladin Verchand, Ankit Pensia, Saminul Haque, Rohith Kuditipudi}\textbf{math.ST}, cs.DS, cs.LG, stat.ML.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16737}{Retrieving Counterfactuals Improves Visual In-Context Learning}{Guangzhi Xiong, Sanchit Sinha, Zhenghao He, Aidong Zhang}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI, cs.CL.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16745}{Persistent Device Identity for Network Access Control in the Era of MAC Address Randomization: A RADIUS-Based Framework}{Premanand Seralathan}\textbf{cs.NI}, cs.CR.

本文针对MAC地址随机化对传统网络访问控制(NAC)的挑战, 提出了一种基于RADIUS协议的持久设备身份框架. 该框架通过RADIUS Access-Accept消息分配并分发Globally Unique Identifier (GUID), 以在设备初始注册、重认证及全生命周期管理中维持身份一致性. 它兼容现有802.1X和MAB基础设施, 无需修改客户端操作系统, 并支持BYOD、托管设备、VPN评估等多种用例, 从而在保护用户隐私的同时满足FISMA、HIPAA等监管要求.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16746}{Data-driven forced response analysis with min-max representations of nonlinear restoring forces}{Akira Saito, Hiromu Fujita}\textbf{math.DS}, cs.LG, nlin.CD.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16781}{IOSVLM: A 3D Vision-Language Model for Unified Dental Diagnosis from Intraoral Scans}{Huimin Xiong, Zijie Meng, Tianxiang Hu, Chenyi Zhou, Yang Feng, Zuozhu Liu}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.

该研究提出了IOSVLM, 一个端到端的3D vision-language model, 用于从intraoral scans (IOS) 点云数据中实现统一的口腔疾病诊断和生成式visual question-answering (VQA). 为了解决无颜色IOS数据与依赖颜色的3D预训练模型之间的分布差距, 作者设计了一个geometry-to-chromatic proxy来稳定细粒度几何感知和跨模态对齐. 模型采用two-stage curriculum training策略增强鲁棒性, 并在新构建的大规模数据集IOSVQA上验证, 在macro accuracy和macro F1 score等指标上显著超越基线方法, 证明了直接建模3D几何对于IOS诊断的有效性.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16792}{V-Co: A Closer Look at Visual Representation Alignment via Co-Denoising}{Han Lin, Xichen Pan, Zun Wang, Yue Zhang, Chu Wang, Jaemin Cho, Mohit Bansal}\textbf{cs.CV}, cs.AI.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16806}{DexGrasp-Zero: A Morphology-Aligned Policy for Zero-Shot Cross-Embodiment Dexterous Grasping}{Yuliang Wu, Yanhan Lin, WengKit Lao, Yuhao Lin, Yi-Lin Wei, Wei-Shi Zheng, Ancong Wu}\textbf{cs.RO}, cs.AI.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16809}{CABTO: Context-Aware Behavior Tree Grounding for Robot Manipulation}{Yishuai Cai, Xinglin Chen, Yunxin Mao, Kun Hu, Minglong Li, Yaodong Yang, Yuanpei Chen}\textbf{cs.RO}, cs.AI.

本文针对机器人操控中Behavior Tree (BT)系统自动化构建的BT Grounding问题, 提出了首个高效求解框架CABTO. 该框架利用预训练Large Models (LMs)在动作模型与控制策略的搜索空间中进行启发式搜索, 并以BT规划器的上下文反馈和环境观测作为引导. 在三个不同机器人操控场景的七组任务实验中, CABTO验证了其在生成完整且一致的BT系统方面的有效性与效率.


\arxivwithtarget{2603.16812}{ODIN-Based CPU-GPU Architecture with Replay-Driven Simulation and Emulation}{Nij Dorairaj, Debabrata Chatterjee, Hong Wang, Hong Jiang, Alankar Saxena, Altug Koker, Thiam Ern Lim, Cathrane Teoh, Chuan Yin Loo, Bishara Shomar, Anthony Lester}\textbf{cs.DC}, cs.AI, cs.AR.



\arxivwithtarget{2603.16825}{Real-Time Decoding of Movement Onset and Offset for Brain-Controlled Rehabilitation Exoskeleton}{Kanishka Mitra, Satyam Kumar, Frigyes Samuel Racz, Deland Liu, Ashish D. Deshpande, José del R. Millán}\textbf{cs.RO}, cs.AI, cs.HC.

本研究提出了一种基于非侵入式EEG的实时双状态运动想象控制方法, 用于驱动上肢康复外骨骼, 实现了运动起始(onset)与终止(offset)的直接脑机控制. 通过引入一种与类别无关的、基于注视点的重定心方法, 有效追踪了EEG信号的漂移, 避免了传统基于任务的重定心方法引入的系统性类别偏差. 该方法显著提升了无阈值分类性能, onset和offset的AUC分别提高了56%和34%, 并减少了日内与日间的偏差. 这些进展将离线解码与实用的、意图驱动的启停控制连接起来, 为符合神经可塑性目标的精准、应变式康复辅助提供了支持.
